<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="right"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">2</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline">Item 1.01 Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">On January 26, 2017, United Continental Holdings, Inc. (&#8220;UAL&#8221;) issued in a public offering $300,000,000 principal amount of its 5.00% Senior Notes due 2024 (the &#8220;Notes&#8221;), which are guaranteed (the &#8220;Guarantee&#8221;) by UAL&#8217;s wholly-owned subsidiary United Airlines, Inc. (&#8220;United&#8221;).&#160;&#160;The Notes and Guarantee were issued pursuant to an Indenture, dated as of May 7, 2013 (the &#8220;Indenture&#8221;), among UAL, United and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as trustee (the &#8220;Trustee&#8221;), as modified and supplemented for purposes of establishing the terms of the Notes by the Third Supplemental Indenture, dated as of January 26, 2017 (the &#8220;Third Supplemental Indenture&#8221;), among UAL, United and the Trustee.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">The Notes will mature on February 1, 2024. The Notes bear interest at a rate of 5.00% per annum, payable semi-annually on February 1 and August 1 of each year, beginning August 1, 2017. The indebtedness evidenced by the Notes may be accelerated upon the occurrence of events of default under the Indenture, as supplemented by the Third Supplemental Indenture, which are customary for securities of this nature. UAL, at its option, may redeem some or all of the Notes at any time at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1) 100% of the principal amount of the Notes being redeemed and (2) a make-whole amount based on the sum of the present values of the remaining scheduled payments of principal and interest on the Notes discounted to the redemption date using a rate based on comparable U.S. Treasury securities plus 50 basis points, plus in either case accrued and unpaid interest to the redemption date.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">The Third Supplemental Indenture is filed herewith as Exhibit 4.2, and is incorporated by reference herein. The form of the Notes and the form of the Notation of Note Guarantee are filed herewith as Exhibits 4.3 and 4.4, respectively, and are incorporated by reference herein. The foregoing descriptions of the Third Supplemental Indenture, the Notes and the Guarantee are qualified in their entirety by reference to such exhibits.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">The issuance of the Notes and the Guarantee was registered pursuant to UAL&#8217;s and United&#8217;s automatic shelf registration statement on Form S-3 (Registration Nos. 333-203630 and 333-203630-1), filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on April 24, 2015.&#160;&#160;The material terms of the Notes and the Guarantee are more fully described in the final Prospectus Supplement, dated January 23, 2017, to the Prospectus, dated April 24, 2015, of UAL and United filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on January 25, 2017 pursuant to Rule 424(b) under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, which description is hereby incorporated herein by reference.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">UNITED CONTINENTAL HOLDINGS, INC.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">5.00% Senior Notes due 2024</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">UNDERWRITING AGREEMENT</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">INCORPORATED</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">As representative of the several underwriters</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;named in Schedule I hereto</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 63pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Incorporated</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">One Bryant Park</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">New York, New York 10036</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Ladies and Gentlemen:</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">United Continental Holdings, Inc., a Delaware corporation (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Company</font>&#8221;), proposes to issue and sell to the several underwriters named in Schedule&#160;I hereto (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Underwriters</font>&#8221;), for whom Merrill Lynch, Pierce, Fenner &amp; Smith Incorporated (&#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Merrill Lynch</font>&#8221; or the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Representative</font>&#8221;) is acting as representative, an aggregate of $300,000,000 principal amount of its 5.00% Senior Notes due 2024 (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Notes</font>&#8221;) on the terms and conditions stated herein.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">The Notes will be issued pursuant to an indenture, dated as of May 7, 2013 (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Base Indenture</font>&#8221;), by and among the Company, United Airlines, Inc. (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Guarantor</font>&#8221;) and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, National Association, as trustee (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Trustee</font>&#8221;), as supplemented by a supplemental indenture to be dated the date of the issuance of the Notes (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;, and together with the Base Indenture, the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Indenture</font>&#8221;), and will be guaranteed by the Guarantor pursuant to the Indenture (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Guarantee</font>&#8221;, and together with the Notes, the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Securities</font>&#8221;).</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">The Company and the Guarantor have filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Commission</font>&#8221;) an automatic shelf registration statement on Form&#160;S-3 (File No. 333-203630) relating to securities, including debt securities and guarantees of debt securities (the &#8220;<font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Shelf Securities</font>&#8221;), to be issued from time to time by the Company and the Guarantor.&#160;&#160;The</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">7.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Default of Underwriters</font>.&#160;&#160;If any Underwriter or Underwriters default in their obligations to purchase Securities hereunder and the aggregate principal amount of the Securities that such defaulting Underwriter or Underwriters agreed but failed to purchase does not exceed 10% of the total principal amount of the Securities, the Representative may make arrangements satisfactory to the Company for the purchase of such Securities by other persons, including any of the non-defaulting Underwriters, but if no such arrangements are made by the Closing Date, the non-defaulting Underwriters shall be obligated severally, in proportion to their respective commitments hereunder, to purchase the Securities that such defaulting Underwriter or Underwriters agreed but failed to purchase.&#160;&#160;If any Underwriter or Underwriters so default and the aggregate principal amount of the Securities with respect to which such default or defaults occurs exceeds 10% of the total principal amount of the Securities and arrangements satisfactory to the Representative and the Company for purchase of such Securities by other persons are not made within 36 hours after such default, this Agreement will terminate without liability on the part of any non-defaulting Underwriter, the Company or the Guarantor, except as provided in Section&#160;6.&#160;&#160;As used in this Agreement, the term &#8220;Underwriter&#8221; includes any person substituted for an Underwriter under this Section.&#160;&#160;Nothing herein will relieve a defaulting Underwriter from liability for its default.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">8.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Survival of Certain Representations and Obligations</font>.&#160;&#160;The respective indemnities, agreements, representations, warranties and other statements of the Company, the Guarantor or their respective officers and of the Underwriters set forth in or made pursuant to this Agreement will remain in full force and effect, regardless of any termination of this Agreement, any investigation, or statement as to the results thereof, made by or on behalf of any Underwriter, the Company, the Guarantor or any of their respective representatives, officers or directors or any controlling person and will survive delivery of and payment for the Securities.&#160;&#160;If for any reason the purchase of the Securities by the Underwriters is not consummated, the Company shall remain responsible for the expenses to be paid or reimbursed by it pursuant to Section&#160;10 hereof and the respective obligations of the Company, the Guarantor and the Underwriters pursuant to Section&#160;6 hereof shall remain in effect.&#160;&#160;If the purchase of the Securities by the Underwriters is not consummated for any reason other than solely because of the occurrence of the termination of the Agreement pursuant to Section&#160;7 or 9 hereof, the Company and the Guarantor will jointly and severally reimburse the Underwriters for all out-of-pocket expenses (including reasonable fees and disbursements of counsel) reasonably incurred by the Underwriters in connection with the offering of such Securities and comply with its obligations under Sections&#160;6 and 10 hereof.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">THIRD SUPPLEMENTAL INDENTURE, dated as of January 26, 2017 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Third Supplemental Indenture</font>&#8221;), among United Continental Holdings, Inc. (&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">UAL</font>&#8221; or the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Issuer</font>&#8221;), United Airlines, Inc. (&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">United</font>&#8221;) and The Bank of New York Mellon Trust Company, N.A., as trustee (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Trustee</font>&#8221;), to the Indenture, dated as of May&#160;7, 2013 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Original Indenture</font>&#8221;), among UAL, United and the Trustee.&#160;&#160;The Original Indenture as supplemented by this Third Supplemental Indenture is hereinafter called the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Indenture</font>.&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">WHEREAS, Section&#160;9.01 of the Original Indenture permits supplements thereto to establish the form or terms of Securities pursuant to Article II of the Original Indenture; and</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">WHEREAS, as contemplated by Section&#160;2.02 of the Original Indenture, UAL wishes to establish the terms of a new Series of Securities (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Notes</font>&#8221;) pursuant to this Third Supplemental Indenture.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">NOW, THEREFORE, this Third Supplemental Indenture witnesseth:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><a name="1"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Section 1.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="1">Defined Terms</a></font>.&#160;&#160;For purposes of this Third Supplemental Indenture, all terms defined in the Original Indenture and used herein have such defined meanings unless otherwise defined herein.&#160;&#160;In addition, Section 7 hereof sets forth certain defined terms for purposes of this Third Supplemental Indenture.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><a name="2"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Section 2.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="2">Relation to Original Indenture</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The Original Indenture is supplemented and modified as set forth in this Third Supplemental Indenture for purposes of the Notes.&#160;&#160;This Third Supplemental Indenture shall not affect any Series of Securities other than the Notes.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><a name="3"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Section 3.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="3">Terms of the Notes</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The terms of the Notes shall be as follows:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="31"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.1</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="31">Issuer</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The issuer of the Notes shall be UAL.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="32"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.2</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="32">Title and Form</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The title of the Notes is 5.00% Senior Notes due 2024.&#160;&#160;The Notes shall be in registered form and in substantially the form attached hereto as <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Exhibit A</font>.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="33"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.3</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="33">Aggregate Principal Amount</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The aggregate principal amount of the Notes which may be authenticated and delivered under the Indenture is initially limited to $300,000,000, except for Notes authenticated and delivered upon registration of transfer of, or in exchange for, or in lieu of, other Notes, and subject to increase as set forth in Section 3.15 hereof.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="34"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.4</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="34">Principal Payment</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The outstanding principal amount of the Notes shall be due and payable on February 1, 2024.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="35"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.5</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="35">Interest</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The outstanding principal amount of the Notes shall bear interest at the rate of 5.00% per annum, payable in arrears on February 1 and August 1 of each year (each, an &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Interest Payment Date</font>&#8221;), commencing on August 1, 2017, to the Persons in whose names the Notes are registered at the close of business on the January 15 and July 15, respectively, next preceding such Interest Payment Date (each, a &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Regular Record Date</font>&#8221;).&#160;&#160;Interest shall accrue from the most recent date to which interest has been paid or for which interest has been provided,</font></div>

<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160; </font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">or, if no interest has been paid or provided for, from January 26, 2017.&#160;&#160;Interest due on any date shall be the amount accrued to but excluding such due date.&#160;&#160;Interest shall be calculated on the basis of a 360-day year of twelve 30-day months.&#160;&#160;Any payment required to be made on any day that is not a Business Day will be made on the next succeeding Business Day without any interest or other payment due to the delay.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="36"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.6</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="36">Method of Payment</a></font>.&#160;&#160;Principal of, premium (if any) and interest on the Notes shall be payable as provided in Section&#160;2.15 of the Original Indenture.&#160;&#160;Notwithstanding the foregoing, payments of principal of, premium (if any) and interest on the Notes represented by one or more Global Notes will be made as provided in Section&#160;3.8 hereof.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="37"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.7</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="37">Optional Redemption</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The Issuer, at its option, may redeem the Notes in whole at any time or in part from time to time, at a redemption price equal to the greater of (1)&#160;100% of the principal amount of the Notes to be redeemed and (2)&#160;the sum of the present values of the remaining scheduled payments of principal and interest on such Notes (excluding accrued and unpaid interest to the redemption date) discounted to the redemption date on a semiannual basis (assuming a 360-day year consisting of twelve 30-day months) at the Treasury Rate (as defined below) plus 50 basis points, plus, in case of either the preceding clause (1) or (2), accrued and unpaid interest on the principal amount being redeemed to such redemption date.&#160;&#160;Article&#160;III of the Original Indenture shall apply to any such redemption, except that the third sentence of Section&#160;3.02 of the Original Indenture shall be amended to read as follows:&#160;&#160;&#8220;Notes and portions thereof that the Trustee selects shall be in principal amounts of $2,000 or integral multiples of $1,000 in excess thereof.&#8221;&#160;&#160;If less than all outstanding Notes are to be redeemed, any selection of Notes to be redeemed shall be subject to applicable procedures of The Depository Trust Company (&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">DTC</font>&#8221;) so long as it is the Depositary.&#160;&#160;For purposes of any redemptions pursuant to this Section 3.7, the following terms shall have the respective specified meanings:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Comparable Treasury Issue</font>&#8221; means the United States Treasury security selected by the Quotation Agent as having a maturity comparable to the remaining term of the Notes to be redeemed that would be utilized, at the time of selection and in accordance with customary financial practice, in pricing new issues of corporate debt securities of comparable maturity to the remaining term of such Notes.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Comparable Treasury Price</font>&#8221; means, with respect to any redemption date for Notes, the average of two Reference Treasury Dealer Quotations for such redemption date.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Quotation Agent</font>&#8221; means the Reference Treasury Dealer appointed by the Issuer.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Reference Treasury Dealer</font>&#8221; means each of Merrill Lynch, Pierce, Fenner &amp; Smith Incorporated and J.P. Morgan Securities LLC, and their respective successors; provided, however, that if any of the foregoing shall cease to be a primary United States Government securities dealer in New York City (a</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<br>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Primary Treasury Dealer</font>&#8221;), the Issuer will substitute therefor another Primary Treasury Dealer.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Reference Treasury Dealer Quotations</font>&#8221; means, with respect to each Reference Treasury Dealer and any redemption date, the average, as determined by the Issuer, of the bid and asked prices for the Comparable Treasury Issue (expressed in each case as a percentage of its principal amount) quoted in writing to the Issuer by such Reference Treasury Dealer at 5:00&#160;p.m., New York City time, on the third Business Day preceding such redemption date.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Treasury Rate</font>&#8221; means, with respect to any redemption date, (1) the yield to maturity calculated by taking the simple average of the yields to maturity for the applicable Comparable Treasury Issue for each of the five Business Days immediately preceding the third Business Day before the calculation date as reported on the most recent H.15 page available through the website of the Board of Governors of the Federal Reserve System at http://www.federalreserve.gov/releases/h15/update, or any successor site or publication, for the applicable Comparable Treasury Issue and which establishes yields on actively traded United States Treasury securities adjusted to constant maturity under the caption &#8220;Treasury Constant Maturities,&#8221; for the maturity corresponding to the Comparable Treasury Issue (if no maturity is within three months before or after the maturity date of the Notes to be redeemed, yields for the two published maturities most closely corresponding to the Comparable Treasury Issue shall be determined, and the Treasury Rate shall be interpolated or extrapolated from such yields on a straight-line basis, rounding to the nearest month) or (2) if such report (or any successor site or publication) is not available during any of such five Business Days or does not contain such yields, the rate per year equal to the semiannual equivalent yield to maturity of the Comparable Treasury Issue, calculated using a price for the Comparable Treasury Issue (expressed as a percentage of its principal amount) equal to the Comparable Treasury Price for such redemption date. The Treasury Rate will be calculated on the third Business Day preceding the redemption date.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="38"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.8</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="38">Global Notes</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The Notes shall initially be issued in the form of one or more Global Securities registered in the name of DTC, which shall be the initial Depositary with respect to the Notes, or its nominee (a &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Global Note</font>&#8221;), which shall be delivered to the Trustee as custodian for the Depositary or its nominee.&#160;&#160;The Paying Agent shall make payments of principal, premium, if any, or interest due on the Notes represented by one or more Global Notes to the Depositary or its nominee, as the case may be, as the registered owner of the related Global Note or Global Notes, by wire transfer of immediately available funds to the account designated by such registered holder.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="39"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.9</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="39">Legends on Notes</a></font>.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(a)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">In addition to the legend set forth in Section 2.14(c) of the Original Indenture, so long as DTC is the Depositary, each Global Note registered in the name of DTC or its nominee shall bear a legend in substantially the following form:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;UNLESS THIS GLOBAL NOTE IS PRESENTED BY AN AUTHORIZED REPRESENTATIVE OF THE DEPOSITORY TRUST COMPANY, A NEW YORK CORPORATION (&#8220;DTC&#8221;), TO THE ISSUER OR ITS AGENT FOR REGISTRATION OF TRANSFER, EXCHANGE OR PAYMENT, AND ANY GLOBAL NOTE ISSUED IS REGISTERED IN THE NAME OF CEDE &amp; CO. OR IN SUCH OTHER NAME AS IS REQUESTED BY AN AUTHORIZED REPRESENTATIVE OF DTC (AND ANY PAYMENT IS MADE TO CEDE &amp; CO. OR TO SUCH OTHER ENTITY AS IS REQUESTED BY AN AUTHORIZED REPRESENTATIVE OF DTC), ANY TRANSFER, PLEDGE OR OTHER USE HEREOF FOR VALUE OR OTHERWISE BY OR TO ANY PERSON IS WRONGFUL INASMUCH THE REGISTERED OWNER HEREOF, CEDE &amp; CO., HAS AN INTEREST HEREIN.&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(b)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">All Notes shall bear a legend substantially in the following form:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;BY ACCEPTANCE OF THIS NOTE OR ANY INTEREST HEREIN, EACH PURCHASER AND SUBSEQUENT TRANSFEREE OF THIS NOTE OR ANY INTEREST HEREIN WILL BE DEEMED TO HAVE REPRESENTED AND WARRANTED TO THE ISSUER AND THE TRUSTEE THAT EITHER (I) SUCH PURCHASER OR TRANSFEREE IS NOT AN EMPLOYEE BENEFIT PLAN THAT IS SUBJECT TO TITLE I OF THE EMPLOYEE RETIREMENT INCOME SECURITY ACT OF 1974, AS AMENDED (&#8220;ERISA&#8221;), A PLAN, INDIVIDUAL RETIREMENT ACCOUNT OR OTHER ARRANGEMENT THAT IS SUBJECT TO SECTION 4975 OF THE INTERNAL REVENUE CODE OF 1986, AS AMENDED (THE &#8220;CODE&#8221;), OR PROVISIONS UNDER ANY FEDERAL, STATE, LOCAL, NON-U.S. OR OTHER LAWS OR REGULATIONS THAT ARE SIMILAR TO SUCH PROVISIONS OF THE CODE OR ERISA (COLLECTIVELY, &#8220;SIMILAR LAWS&#8221;), OR AN ENTITY WHOSE UNDERLYING ASSETS ARE CONSIDERED TO INCLUDE &#8220;PLAN ASSETS&#8221; OF SUCH PLANS, ACCOUNTS AND ARRANGEMENTS (COLLECTIVELY, &#8220;PLANS&#8221;), AND NO PORTION OF THE ASSETS USED BY SUCH PURCHASER OR TRANSFEREE TO ACQUIRE AND HOLD THIS NOTE OR ANY INTEREST HEREIN CONSTITUTES ASSETS OF ANY PLAN OR (II) THE PURCHASE AND HOLDING OF THIS NOTE OR ANY INTEREST HEREIN BY SUCH PURCHASER OR TRANSFEREE WILL NOT CONSTITUTE A NON-EXEMPT PROHIBITED TRANSACTION UNDER SECTION 406 OF ERISA OR SECTION 4975 OF THE CODE OR A VIOLATION OF ANY APPLICABLE SIMILAR LAW.&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="310"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.10</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="310">Note Denominations</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The Notes shall be issued in denominations of $2,000 or an integral multiple of $1,000 in excess thereof.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="311"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.11</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="311">No Sinking Fund</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The Notes will not be entitled to the benefit of any sinking fund.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="312"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.12</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="312">Indenture Covenants</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The covenants set forth in Article IV and Article V of the Original Indenture shall apply to the Notes.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="313"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.13</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="313">Note Guarantee</a></font>.&#160;&#160;United (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Guarantor</font>&#8221;) fully and unconditionally guarantees the Notes pursuant to Article&#160;X of the Original Indenture (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Note Guarantee</font>&#8221;).</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">The Notation of Note Guarantee substantially in the form attached hereto as <font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Exhibit&#160;B</font> shall be executed by United and attached to each Note authenticated pursuant to the Indenture.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="314"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.14</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="314">Amendments</a></font>.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(a)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Section 9.01(1) of the Original Indenture shall be amended to insert the following at the end thereof:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;, or to evidence the succession of another Person to the Guarantor pursuant to Section 10.04 and the assumption by such successor of the Guarantor&#8217;s covenants, agreements and obligations in this Indenture and with respect to the Securities;&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(b)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;S</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">ection 9.02(7) of the Original Indenture shall be amended and restated to read as follows:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#8220;except as provided under Article VIII hereof or in connection with a consolidation, merger or conveyance, transfer or lease of assets pursuant to this Indenture, release any Securities Guarantor from any of its obligations under its Securities Guarantee or make any change in a Securities Guarantee that would adversely affect such Holder; or&#8221;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;</font><a name="315">3.15</a></font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt"><a name="315">&#160;</a></font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="315">Further Issuances</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The Issuer may, from time to time, without notice to or the consent of the Holders of the Notes, increase the principal amount of the Notes under the Indenture and issue such increased principal amount (or any portion thereof), in which case any additional Notes so issued will have the same form and terms (other than the date of issuance and, under certain circumstances, the date from which interest thereon will begin to accrue), and will carry the same right to receive accrued and unpaid interest, as the Notes previously issued, and such additional Notes will form a single series with the Notes.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="316"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">3.16</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="316">No Reissuance of Notes</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The Issuer may not reissue a Note that has matured, been redeemed, been purchased by the Issuer at the Holder&#8217;s option upon a Change of Control or otherwise been canceled, except for registration of transfer, exchange or replacement of such Note.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><a name="4"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Section 4.</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="4">Additional Covenants Applicable to the Notes</a></font>.&#160;&#160;The following covenants shall be applicable for purposes of the Notes:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="41"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">4.1</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline">Offer to Repurchase Upon Change of Control</font>.</font></a></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(a)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Upon the occurrence of a Change of Control, each Holder of Notes shall have the right to require the Issuer to repurchase all or any part (equal to $2,000 or an integral multiple of $1,000 in excess thereof) of that Holder&#8217;s Notes pursuant to an offer (a &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Change of Control Offer</font>&#8221;) at a purchase price in cash equal to 101% of the aggregate principal amount of Notes repurchased, plus accrued and unpaid interest on the Notes repurchased to the date of purchase (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Change of Control Payment</font>&#8221;), subject to the rights of Holders of Notes on the relevant Record Date to receive interest due on the relevant Interest Payment Date.&#160;&#160;Within 30 days</font></div>

<br>
<div id="PGBRK" style="WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160; </font></div>
</div>

<div id="PN" style="WIDTH: 100%; PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always">
<div style="WIDTH: 100%; TEXT-ALIGN: center"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">5</font></div>

<hr style="COLOR: black" noshade size="2">
</div>

<div id="HDR">
<div id="GLHDR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="right"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160; </font></div>
</div>
</div>

<br>
<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">following any Change of Control, the Issuer shall mail a notice to each Holder describing the transaction or transactions that constitute the Change of Control and stating:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>(1)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;that the Change of Control Offer is being made pursuant to this Section 4.1 and that all Notes tendered will be accepted for payment;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>(2)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the purchase price and the purchase date, which shall be no earlier than 30 days and no later than 60 days from the date such notice is mailed (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Change of Control Payment Date</font>&#8221;);</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>(3)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;that any Note not tendered will continue to accrue interest;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>(4)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;that, unless the Issuer defaults in the payment of the Change of Control Payment, all Notes accepted for payment pursuant to the Change of Control Offer will cease to accrue interest after the Change of Control Payment Date;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>(5)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;that Holders of Notes electing to have any Notes purchased pursuant to a Change of Control Offer will be required to surrender the Notes, with the form entitled &#8220;Option of Holder to Elect Purchase&#8221; attached to the Notes completed, or transfer such Notes by book-entry transfer, to the Paying Agent at the address specified in the notice prior to the close of business on the third Business Day preceding the Change of Control Payment Date;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>(6)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;that Holders of Notes will be entitled to withdraw their election if the Paying Agent receives, not later than the close of business on the second Business Day preceding the Change of Control Payment Date, a telegram, telex, facsimile transmission or letter setting forth the name of the Holder, the principal amount of Notes delivered for purchase, and a statement that such Holder is withdrawing its election to have the Notes purchased; and</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>(7)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;that Holders of Notes whose Notes are being purchased only in part will be issued new Notes equal in principal amount to the unpurchased portion of the Notes surrendered, which unpurchased portion must be equal to $2,000 in principal amount or an integral multiple of $1,000 in excess thereof.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font id="TAB1" style="MARGIN-LEFT: 36pt"></font>The Issuer will comply with the requirements of Rule 14e-1 under the Exchange Act and any other securities laws and regulations thereunder to the extent those laws and regulations are applicable in connection with the repurchase of the Notes as a result of a Change of Control.&#160;&#160;To the extent that the provisions of any securities laws or regulations conflict with the provisions of this Section&#160;4.1, the Issuer will comply with the applicable securities laws and regulations and will not be deemed to have breached its obligations under this Section&#160;4.1 by virtue of such compliance.&#160;&#160;The Issuer will provide a copy of such notice to the Trustee.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(b)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">On the Change of Control Payment Date, the Issuer will, to the extent lawful:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><br>
<div id="PGBRK" style="WIDTH: 100%; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt">
<div id="FTR">
<div id="GLFTR" style="WIDTH: 100%" align="left"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 8pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160; </font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(1)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;accept for payment all Notes or portions of Notes properly tendered pursuant to the Change of Control Offer;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(2)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;deposit with the Paying Agent an amount equal to the Change of Control Payment in respect of all Notes or portions of Notes properly tendered; and</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(3)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;deliver or cause to be delivered to the Trustee the Notes properly accepted together with an Officers&#8217; Certificate stating the aggregate principal amount of Notes or portions of Notes being purchased by the Issuer.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">The Paying Agent will promptly mail (or pay by wire transfer) (but in any case not later than five days after the Change of Control Payment Date) to each Holder of Notes properly tendered the Change of Control Payment for such Notes, and the Issuer shall issue, and the Trustee will promptly authenticate and mail (or cause to be transferred by book entry) to each such Holder a new Note equal in principal amount to any unpurchased portion of the Notes surrendered, if any.&#160;&#160;The Issuer will publicly announce the results of the Change of Control Offer on or as soon as practicable after the Change of Control Payment Date.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(c)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">Notwithstanding anything to the contrary in this Indenture or the Notes:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(1)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the Issuer shall not be required to make a Change of Control Offer upon a Change of Control if (1) a third party makes the Change of Control Offer in the manner, at the times and otherwise in compliance with the requirements set forth in this Section&#160;4.1 and purchases all Notes properly tendered and not withdrawn under the Change of Control Offer or (2) notice of redemption with respect to all Notes has been given pursuant to Section 3.01 of the Indenture, unless and until there is a default in payment of the applicable redemption price; and</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(2)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;a Change of Control Offer may be made in advance of a Change of Control, conditioned upon the consummation of such Change of Control, if a definitive agreement is in place for the Change of Control at the time the Change of Control Offer is made.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(d)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">For the avoidance of doubt, the Issuer&#8217;s failure to make a Change of Control Offer would constitute a Default under clause (3) of Section 6.01 of the Indenture and not clause (1) or (2) thereof, but the failure of the Issuer to pay the Change of Control Payment when due shall constitute a Default under clause (1) of Section 6.01 thereof.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><a name="42"><!--EFPlaceholder--><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">4.2</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font></a><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline"><font style="TEXT-DECORATION: underline; DISPLAY: inline"><a name="42">Restricted Payments</a></font>.</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(a)</font><font id="TAB2" style="COLOR: black; LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">The Issuer shall not, and shall not permit any of its Restricted Subsidiaries to, directly or indirectly:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(1)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;declare or pay any dividend or make any other payment or distribution on account of the Issuer&#8217;s or any of its Restricted Subsidiaries&#8217; Equity</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(2)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;purchase, redeem or otherwise acquire or retire for value any Equity Interests of the Issuer;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(3)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;make any payment on or with respect to, or purchase, redeem, defease or otherwise acquire or retire for value (collectively for purposes of this clause (3), a &#8220;purchase&#8221;) any Indebtedness of the Issuer or the Guarantor that is contractually subordinated to the Notes or the Note Guarantee (excluding any intercompany Indebtedness between or among the Issuer and any of its Restricted Subsidiaries), except any scheduled payment of interest and any purchase within two years of the Scheduled Maturity thereof; or</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(4)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;make any Restricted Investment (all such payments and other actions set forth in these clauses (1) through (4) above being collectively referred to as &#8220;<font style="FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-STYLE: italic; DISPLAY: inline">Restricted Payments</font>&#8221;),</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">unless, at the time of and after giving effect to such Restricted Payment:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 108pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(i)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;no Default has occurred and is continuing;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 108pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(ii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the Issuer would, at the time of such Restricted Payment and after giving pro forma effect thereto as if such Restricted Payment had been made at the beginning of the applicable four-quarter period, have been permitted to incur at least $1.00 of additional Indebtedness pursuant to the Fixed Charge Coverage Ratio test set forth in Section 4.3(a) hereof; and</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 108pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(iii)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;such Restricted Payment, together with the aggregate amount of all other Restricted Payments made by the Issuer and its Restricted Subsidiaries since the Closing Date (excluding Restricted Payments permitted by clauses (2) through (20) of Section 4.2(b) hereof) is less than the sum, without duplication, of:</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 144pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(A)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;50% of the Consolidated Net Income of the Issuer for the period (taken as one accounting period) from July 1, 2011, to the end of the Issuer&#8217;s most recently ended fiscal quarter for which internal financial statements are available at the time of such Restricted Payment (or, if such Consolidated Net Income for such period is a deficit, less 100% of such deficit); plus</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(12)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the distribution, as a dividend or otherwise, of shares of Capital Stock of, or Indebtedness owed to the Issuer or any of its Restricted Subsidiaries by, any Unrestricted Subsidiary;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(13)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the distribution or dividend of assets or Capital Stock of any Person in connection with any full or partial &#8220;spin-off&#8221; of a Subsidiary or similar transactions; provided that (i) the Issuer would, on the date of such distribution after giving pro forma effect thereto as if the same had occurred at the beginning of the applicable four-quarter period, be permitted to incur at least $1.00 of additional Indebtedness pursuant to the Fixed Charge Coverage Ratio test set forth in Section 4.3(a) hereof, (ii) such pro forma Fixed Charge Coverage Ratio referred to in the preceding clause (i) would be greater than or equal to such Fixed Charge Coverage Ratio immediately prior to such transaction or (iii) if such Subsidiary is not the Guarantor, no Default has occurred and is continuing;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(14)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the distribution or dividend of assets or Capital Stock of any Person in connection with any full or partial &#8220;spin-off&#8221; of a Subsidiary or similar transactions having an aggregate Fair Market Value not to exceed $500.0 million since the Closing Date;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(15)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;so long as no Default has occurred and is continuing, other Restricted Payments in an aggregate amount not to exceed $1.0 billion, such aggregate amount to be calculated from the Closing Date;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(16)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;so long as no Default has occurred and is continuing, any Restricted Investment by the Issuer and/or any Restricted Subsidiary of the Issuer;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(17)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;the payment of any amounts in respect of any restricted stock units or other instruments or rights whose value is based in whole or in part on the value of any Equity Interests issued to any directors, officers or employees of the Issuer or any Restricted Subsidiary of the Issuer;</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(18)&#160;&#160;so long as no Default has occurred and is continuing, Restricted Payments (i) made to purchase or redeem Equity Interests of Issuer or (ii) consisting of payments in respect of any Indebtedness (whether for purchase or prepayment thereof or otherwise);</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">&#160;(19)&#160;&#160;any Restricted Payment so long as both before and after giving effect to such Restricted Payment, Issuer and its Restricted Subsidiaries have Liquidity in the aggregate of at least $2.2 billion; and</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 72pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(20)&#160;&#160;Restricted Payments in an aggregate amount which do not exceed 5.0% of the Consolidated Tangible Assets of Issuer and its Restricted Subsidiaries (calculated at the time of such Restricted Payment).</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 72pt" align="justify"><font style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman; DISPLAY: inline">(c)&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;In the case of any Restricted Payment that is not cash, the amount of such non-cash Restricted Payment will be the Fair Market Value on the date of the Restricted</font></div>

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
